This means the business initially has to ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"spend extra cash"}]," (the VAT amount), which affects its ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"cash flow"}]," until the VAT is refunded or offset against future sales. "]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":["Where if the second transaction is smaller (selling for NPR 50,000 with a VAT of NPR 6,500), the business can reclaim the ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"input VAT"}]," (NPR 13,000) up to the ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"output VAT"}]," it collects (NPR 6,500). "]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":"The business can reclaim this carried-forward VAT against future sales where it collects more output VAT."}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":["If the business cannot offset the remaining ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"NPR 6,500"}]," input VAT against future sales, it can apply for a ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"VAT refund"}],"."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":["This typically happens when:\n",["$","ul",null,{"className":"x:[:is(ol,ul)_&]:my-3 x:not-first:mt-6 x:list-disc x:ms-6","children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":"The business stops operations or completes its current cycle."}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":"Input VAT exceeds output VAT due to circumstances like lower sales or no sales at all."}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":["The refund process usually involves:\n",["$","ol",null,{"className":"x:[:is(ol,ul)_&]:my-3 x:not-first:mt-6 x:list-decimal x:ms-6","children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":"Filing a VAT return showing the excess input VAT."}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":"Submitting the necessary supporting documents, such as purchase invoices and sales records."}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":"Awaiting verification and approval from the tax authorities."}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"4.
